# FORGE Basketball Coach Review Sample Pack

**Generated**: 2026-06-23  
**Generator**: `scripts/generate_coach_review_samples.py`  
**Purpose**: External S&C coach review — 18 samples across 3 roles × 3 levels

## How to Use This Pack

1. Review the **Coverage Matrix** below to understand the scope.
2. Each **role × level** section contains two samples (A and B).
3. Each sample includes: athlete profile, rationale, full program, exposure summary.
4. At the end of each sample, use the **Coach Review Prompts** to guide your feedback.
5. Record your overall feedback in the separate **Review Sheet** (`*_review_sheet.md`).

| Role | Level | Variant A | Variant B |
|---|---|---|---|
| Guard | Beginner | `BASKETBALL_GUARD_BEGINNER_A` | `BASKETBALL_GUARD_BEGINNER_B` |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Guard** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 0.5 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.YOUTH_FOUNDATION — Build movement literacy, general strength, and athleticism. No specialisation. Fun + competence.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 0-2 years
- **Role week note**: Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Youth Foundation (U14-U20) (ID: 7)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: guard
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 2x/week — 16 total sessions

### Coach Review Prompts

- [ ] Does this **Guard (Beginner)** program feel role-appropriate?
- [ ] Is the weekly training frequency appropriate for this athlete archetype?
- [ ] Are exercise selections and sequencing coach-like and sport-relevant?
- [ ] Does the conditioning density match the sport's physiological demands?
- [ ] Is the loading / intensity progression realistic for this level?
- [ ] What is the single most impactful change you would make?
- [ ] Would you trust this program with a real athlete at this level?

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Guard** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.

|---|---|
| **Blueprint** | Sprint Development |
| **Duration** | 8 weeks |
| **Frequency** | 3x/week |
| **Conditioning Emphasis** | Pre Season — Speed |
| **Competition Window** | Off-season |
| **Role Emphasis** | guard — basketball |
| **Credibility Score** | 0.96 |

### Block Overview (Week-by-Week)

```
BLOCK SUMMARY
============================================================
basketball Athlete (speed)
Blueprint: Sprint Development | Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Basic Gym
Program Score: 1.0/1.0 (96%)

Personalization:
  Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

 Wk | Intent             | Tests                          | Adj | Notes
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
W 1 | accumulation       | Jump / Power, Movement / Techn |     | 
W 2 | accumulation       |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 3 | intensification    |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 4 | intensification    |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 5 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 6 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 7 | taper              |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 8 | deload             |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families

Exposure by Week:
  W1 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W2 (accumulation        ): 15 ex | 3 sqt 0 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W3 (intensification     ): 15 ex | 3 sqt 0 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W4 (intensification     ): 15 ex | 3 sqt 0 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W5 (intensification     ): 15 ex | 3 sqt 0 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W6 (peak                ): 15 ex | 3 sqt 0 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W7 (taper               ): 15 ex | 3 sqt 0 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W8 (deload              ): 15 ex | 3 sqt 0 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot

  Role Exposure Targets:
    Sprint:        High  | Jump/Landing: Moderate
    Deceleration:  High  | Rotation:     Low
    Conditioning:  High

Role Week Bias:
  Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

Role Weekly Emphasis Targets:
  Force emphasis:           0.3
  Velocity emphasis:        0.8
  Conditioning emphasis:    0.7
  Rotation emphasis:        0.4
  Landing emphasis:         0.5
  Upper-body emphasis:      0.5

  Sprint exposure target:   High
  Jump/Landing exposure target: Moderate
  Deceleration exposure target: High
  Rotation exposure target: Low
  Conditioning density:     High

Testing / Benchmarking:
  Week 1: Movement / Technical Benchmark, Jump / Power Test
  Week 5: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test
  Week 6: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test

============================================================
```

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [Sprint] Sprint
    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3 x 15-20m  |  technique focus  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [Plyo] Plyo
    - Pogo Jump  2-3 x 4-6  |  quality, 2-3s reset, conservative lower-complexity plyo  |  rest: 90s
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Air Squat  2-3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 3:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - Glute Bridge  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [HPull] HPull
    - Scapular Retraction  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  2-3 x 20-30s holds / 8-12 reps  |  quality, brace  |  rest: 45s
  Conditioning: 10m Acceleration
    10m maximal acceleration from 2-point or 3-point start.
  Est. time: 40 min
```

### Weekly Exposure Summary

| Week | Sprint | Jump/Landing | Decel | Eccentric | Cond. Density | Type |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.SPRINT_DEVELOPMENT — Max velocity and/or acceleration improvement. Strength underpins but speed is priority.

- **Role week note**: Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Guard** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.COURT_SPORT_AD — Multi-directional power, deceleration, change of direction, and lateral strength.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 1-5 years
- **Role week note**: Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Court Sport Athletic Development (ID: 8)

- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: guard

- Represents a **intermediate Guard** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test

    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3-4 x 20-30m  |  build to max  |  rest: 2:30 min
  [Plyo] Plyo
    - Squat Jump  3 x 4-6  |  max intent  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-9  |  rest: 4:00 min

    - RDL  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-9  |  rest: 4:00 min

  [Core] Core
    - Plank  3 x 30-45s holds / 10-15 reps  |  quality, anti-movement  |  rest: 45s
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.SPRINT_DEVELOPMENT — Max velocity and/or acceleration improvement. Strength underpins but speed is priority.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season, in_season | **Best training age**: 2-5 years
- **Role week note**: Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Sprint Development (ID: 10)
- **Rationale**: Goal: speed | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: guard
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Guard** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
```

- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Guard** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Guard role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [HPush] HPush
    - Barbell Bench Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [HPull] HPull
    - Dumbbell Row  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [VPush] VPush
    - Barbell Overhead Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 2:00 min
```

- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Wing** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 0.8 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.7
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.5
-   Landing emphasis:         0.6
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.6
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Moderate
-   Deceleration exposure target: Moderate
-   Rotation exposure target: Moderate
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

```
basketball Athlete (conditioning)
```

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

| Week | Sprint | Jump/Landing | Decel | Eccentric | Cond. Density | Type |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Week 1 | Moderate (3 ex, 16.7%) | None (0 ex, 0.0%) | None (0 ex, 0.0%) | Moderate (3 ex, 16.7%) | Moderate (3 ex, 16.7%) | accumulation |
| Week 2 | Moderate (3 ex, 16.7%) | None (0 ex, 0.0%) | None (0 ex, 0.0%) | Moderate (3 ex, 16.7%) | Moderate (3 ex, 16.7%) | accumulation |

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.STRENGTH_CONDITIONING — Strength maintenance + energy system development. Common in pre-season / GPP blocks.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season | **Best training age**: 1-4 years
- **Role week note**: Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Strength + Conditioning (ID: 3)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: wing
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [Sprint] Sprint
    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3-4 x 20-30m  |  build to max  |  rest: 2:30 min
  [Ball] Ball
    - Med Ball Slam  3-4 x 3-5  |  explosive, RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:30 min
  [HPush] HPush
    - Barbell Bench Press  3 x 8-10  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  [SLKD] SLKD
    - Bulgarian Split Squat  3 x 8-10  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s

    - Rotational Med Ball Wall Slam  3 x 3-5  |  explosive, RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  3 x 30-45s holds / 10-15 reps  |  quality, anti-movement  |  rest: 45s
```

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Wing** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.STRENGTH_CONDITIONING — Strength maintenance + energy system development. Common in pre-season / GPP blocks.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season | **Best training age**: 1-4 years
- **Role week note**: Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Strength + Conditioning (ID: 3)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: wing
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Wing** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Wing** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Wing role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Advanced
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: wing
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

# Big — Beginner

## Sample: BASKETBALL_BIG_BEGINNER_A

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `BASKETBALL_BIG_BEGINNER_A` |
| **Sport** | Basketball |
| **Role** | Big |
| **Level** | Beginner |
| **Age** | 16 |
| **Training Age** | 0.5 years |
| **Goal** | Strength |
| **Days/Week** | 2 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Off Season |
| **Equipment** | Basic Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.7 |
| **Strength Base Met** | No |
| **Blueprint** | Youth Foundation (U14-U20) |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Big** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 0.5 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Strength** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.8
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.4
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.5

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (strength)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Lateral shuffle (dynamic) (0 min)
      Cue: Stay low, don't cross feet
    - Crossover run (0 min)
      Cue: Rotate hips, drive across body
  Activate (5 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - Split-step prep (0 min)
      Cue: Load hips, light jump, land soft
    - Reactive shuffle (0 min)
      Cue: Low stance, quick feet, react to signal
    - Lunge-recover pattern (0 min)
      Cue: Push off front foot, recover to stance
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Sub-max squat (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Stand fast, controlled descent

    - Air Squat  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 3:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - Glute Bridge  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.YOUTH_FOUNDATION — Build movement literacy, general strength, and athleticism. No specialisation. Fun + competence.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 0-2 years
- **Role week note**: Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Youth Foundation (U14-U20) (ID: 7)
- **Rationale**: Goal: strength | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: big
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 2x/week — 16 total sessions

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Big** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 0.8 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

```
  Landing emphasis:         0.7
  Upper-body emphasis:      0.6

  Sprint exposure target:   Low
  Jump/Landing exposure target: High
  Deceleration exposure target: Low
  Rotation exposure target: Low
  Conditioning density:     Moderate

Testing / Benchmarking:
  Week 1: Movement / Technical Benchmark, Jump / Power Test
  Week 5: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test
  Week 6: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test

============================================================
```

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: big
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

### Coach Review Prompts

- [ ] Does this **Big (Beginner)** program feel role-appropriate?
- [ ] Is the weekly training frequency appropriate for this athlete archetype?
- [ ] Are exercise selections and sequencing coach-like and sport-relevant?
- [ ] Does the conditioning density match the sport's physiological demands?
- [ ] Is the loading / intensity progression realistic for this level?
- [ ] What is the single most impactful change you would make?
- [ ] Would you trust this program with a real athlete at this level?

# Big — Intermediate

## Sample: BASKETBALL_BIG_INTERMEDIATE_A

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `BASKETBALL_BIG_INTERMEDIATE_A` |
| **Sport** | Basketball |
| **Role** | Big |
| **Level** | Intermediate |
| **Age** | 20 |
| **Training Age** | 2.0 years |
| **Goal** | Strength |
| **Days/Week** | 3 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Off Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Court Sport Athletic Development |
| **Credibility Score** | 0.93 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Big** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Strength** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.8
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.4
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.5
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.7
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.6
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Low
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: High
-   Deceleration exposure target: Low
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

```
BLOCK SUMMARY
============================================================
basketball Athlete (strength)
Blueprint: Court Sport Athletic Development | Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks

Program Score: 0.9/1.0 (93%)

W 3 | intensification    |                                |     |

W 5 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |     | 
W 6 | accumulation       | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families; High sprint volume; light conditioning; Downgraded realization to accumulation
W 7 | taper              |                                |     | 
W 8 | test               | Conditioning Benchmark, Lower  |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families; High sprint volume; light conditioning
```

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (strength)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Lateral shuffle (dynamic) (0 min)
      Cue: Stay low, don't cross feet
    - Crossover run (0 min)
      Cue: Rotate hips, drive across body
  Activate (5 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - Split-step prep (0 min)
      Cue: Load hips, light jump, land soft
    - Reactive shuffle (0 min)
      Cue: Low stance, quick feet, react to signal
    - Lunge-recover pattern (0 min)
      Cue: Push off front foot, recover to stance
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Sub-max squat (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Stand fast, controlled descent
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.COURT_SPORT_AD — Multi-directional power, deceleration, change of direction, and lateral strength.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 1-5 years
- **Role week note**: Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Court Sport Athletic Development (ID: 8)
- **Rationale**: Goal: strength | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: big
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Big** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.8
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.4
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.5
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.7
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.6
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Low
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: High
-   Deceleration exposure target: Low
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-9  |  rest: 4:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-9  |  rest: 4:00 min

    - Dumbbell Row  3 x 8-10  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s

    - Standing DB Press  3 x 8-10  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: big
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 26 |
| **Training Age** | 5.0 years |
| **Goal** | Strength |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Big** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Strength** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.8
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.4
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.5
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.7
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.6
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Low
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: High
-   Deceleration exposure target: Low
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (strength)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Lateral shuffle (dynamic) (0 min)
      Cue: Stay low, don't cross feet
    - Crossover run (0 min)
      Cue: Rotate hips, drive across body
  Activate (5 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - Split-step prep (0 min)
      Cue: Load hips, light jump, land soft
    - Reactive shuffle (0 min)
      Cue: Low stance, quick feet, react to signal
    - Lunge-recover pattern (0 min)
      Cue: Push off front foot, recover to stance
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Sub-max squat (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Stand fast, controlled descent
```

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years

- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role

| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 30 |
| **Training Age** | 7.0 years |
| **Goal** | Power |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 75 min |
| **Season Phase** | In Season |
| **Equipment** | Elite Facility |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Big** athlete in the **basketball** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

- Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias

- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

### Full Program Output

```
basketball Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Big role -> maximal force / jump-landing emphasis / collision robustness bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [HPush] HPush
    - Barbell Bench Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [HPull] HPull
    - Dumbbell Row  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [VPush] VPush
    - Barbell Overhead Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8, power bias / explosive execution  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  3 x 45-60s holds / 12-15 reps  |  quality, anti-movement  |  rest: 45s
  Conditioning: Court Sport RSA — 5m Shuttle
    5 × 5m shuttles (touch and go, 4 direction changes). One rep = 25m total distance.
  Est. time: 40 min

--- W1 S2 (accumulation) ---
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
